This will allow you to add your family 's expenses to figure out if your little brother is laundering money ( perhaps literally ) . Have fun ! Common Core Standard : 5.NBT.B.7Adding decimals Practice : Add decimals 1 Practice : Add decimals 2 Practice : Add decimals 3 Practice : Add decimals 4 Practice : Add decimals 5 Practice : Add decimals 6 Adding decimals : standard algorithm Honestly , once you remember one very important rule , the rest of adding and subtracting decimals is a snap . That rule is to be sure and align your decimals first . In this tutorial , you 'll get a chance to practice this with us and become fluent adding decimals . Let 's practice ! If you precisely measure anything , you 're likely to get a decimal . If you do n't know how to multiply these decimals , then you wo n't be able to do all the powerful things that multiplication can do in the real world ( figure out your commission as a robot possum salesperson , determining how much shag carpet you need for your secret lair , etc . ) .Intro to multiplying decimals Multiplying decimals : place value Multiplying decimals ( no standard algorithm ) Practice : Multiply decimals 1 Practice : Multiply decimals 2 Practice : Multiply decimals 3 Multiplying decimals : standard algorithm You 've already multiplied decimals in the 5th grade . Solve problems like 30.24 divided by 0.42.Dividing decimals with hundredths Dividing decimals completely Long division with decimals Practice : Dividing decimals : hundredths Dividing by a multi-digit decimal Practice : Dividing decimals : ten thousandths Significant figuresThere is a strong temptation in life to appear precise , even when you are are n't accurate . If you precisely measure one dimension of a carpet to be 3.256 meters and eyeball the other dimensional to be `` roughly 2 meters '' , can you really claim that the area is 6.512 square meters ( 3.256 x 2 ) ? Is n't that a little misleading ? \n\nThis tutorial gets us thinking about this conundrum and gives us the best practices that scientists and engineers use to not mislead each other.Intro to significant figures Rules of significant figures Addition and subtraction with significant figures Multiplying and dividing with significant figures Practice : Significant figures PracticeFractions\n\n\n \n \n\n \n \n $ LAB.queueWait ( function ( ) { window.PackageManager = window.PackageManager || { \n _q : [ ] , \n markExecuted : function ( ) { \n this._q.push.apply ( this._q , arguments ) ; \n } \n } ; \nPackageManager.markExecuted ( `` shared-minimal.css '' ) } ) \n $ LAB.queueScript ( \'https : //cdn.kastatic.org/genfiles/javascript/en/corelibs-package-085b94.js\ ' ) \n $ LAB.queueWait ( function ( ) { PackageManager.markExecuted ( `` corelibs.js '' ) } ) \n\n $ LAB.queueScript ( \'https : //cdn.kastatic.org/genfiles/javascript/en/shared-package-6339db.js\ ' ) \n $ LAB.queueWait ( function ( ) { PackageManager.markExecuted ( `` shared.js '' ) } ) \n\n $ LAB.queueWait ( function ( ) { KAdefine.require ( `` ./javascript/shared-package/site-infra.js '' ) .init ( ) ; } ) \n \n\n \n \n \n \n\n $ LAB.queueWait ( function ( ) { KAdefine.updatePathToPackageMap ( { `` javascript/node_modules/react-dom/index.js '' : `` corelibs.js '' , `` javascript/node_modules/react/index.js '' : `` corelibs.js '' , `` javascript/page-package/footer.jsx '' : `` page.js '' } ) } ) \n\n \n $ LAB.queueWait ( function ( ) { \n var KA = KAdefine.require ( `` ./javascript/shared-package/ka.js '' ) ; \n\n var isDesktopSize = window.innerWidth > 768 ; \n var isContentPage = `` '' ; \n var isMobile = KA.featureFlag ( \'isMobile\ ' ) ; \n\n // Note : we also hide the footer for tablet exercises .
